GT Equivalence Verification (CRK35)
============================================================
GT: -c0*A + c1*_q*A*log(c2*t + c3)
Candidate formulas: 87

GT is the fixed function
\[
f(t,A)=A\Big(\alpha\log(\beta t+1)-\gamma\Big)
\]
with \(\alpha=0.062258070344434831\), \(\beta=0.9423435234237035\), \(\gamma=0.13625696690019862\).
So GT is (i) linear in \(A\) (no \(|A|\), no \(A^2\), no nonlinear \(A\)-dependence), (ii) has exactly one \(\log(\beta t+1)\) term multiplied by \(A\), and (iii) has no extra additive terms independent of \(A\).

Below, each candidate matches iff we can set its free constants to make it exactly \(A(k_1\log(k_2 t+1)+k_0)\) with no other surviving terms.

---

### 1.
\(A c0 (c1+t)^{c2} + c3 e^{c4 t} + c5|A|\).  
Has power in \(t\), exponential term independent of \(A\), and \(|A|\). Cannot become \(A\log(\cdot)+A\) for all \(t,A\). **No**.

### 2.
\(A c0/(c1+t)^{1/4} + A c2 + A c3(c4+t)^{c5}\).  
Only powers/rational powers in \(t\), no log. Cannot equal \(A\log(\beta t+1)\) for all \(t\). **No**.

### 3.
\(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1) + A c3\).  
Combine constants: \(A(c1\log(c2 t+1) + (c0+c3))\). This has the exact GT form. Choose:
- \(c1=\alpha\)
- \(c2=\beta\)
- \(c0+c3=-\gamma\) (e.g., \(c0=-\gamma, c3=0\)).  
**Yes, matches.**

### 4.
\(c0|A| + c1\log(c2 t+1)|A|\).  
Uses \(|A|\) not \(A\). Cannot equal GT for negative \(A\). **No**.

### 5.
\(A c0 + c1\log(c2 t+1)|A|\).  
Second term uses \(|A|\). Cannot match for negative \(A\) unless \(c1=0\), but then no log term. **No**.

### 6.
\(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)\).  
Exactly \(A(c1\log(c2 t+1)+c0)\). Choose:
- \(c1=\alpha\)
- \(c2=\beta\)
- \(c0=-\gamma\).  
**Yes, matches.**

### 7.
\(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1) + c3\log(c4 t+1)\).  
Extra log term independent of \(A\). Must set \(c3=0\) to remove it, then reduces to candidate 6 which can match. **Yes, matches (set \(c3=0\) and as in #6).**

### 8.
\(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1) + A c3(c4+t)^{c5}\).  
Extra \(A\cdot (c4+t)^{c5}\) term. Must set \(c3=0\), then reduces to #6. **Yes, matches (set \(c3=0\) and as in #6).**

### 9.
\(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1) + A c3(c4 t+1)^{c5}\).  
Extra \(A\cdot(\text{power})\) term. Set \(c3=0\) → #6. **Yes, matches.**

### 10.
\(A c0 + A c1 e^{c2 t} + c3 + c4(c5+t)^{c6}\max(0,A)\).  
Has exponential in \(t\) instead of log, plus \(\max(0,A)\) nonlinearity and constant term. Cannot become GT. **No**.

### 11.
\(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1) + c3\).  
Extra constant independent of \(A\). Must set \(c3=0\), then #6. **Yes, matches.**

### 12.
\(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1) + A c3 + c4\).  
Need \(c4=0\) (no constant term). Then \(A(c1\log(\cdot)+(c0+c3))\) which can match by choosing \(c1,c2\) and \(c0+c3=-\gamma\). **Yes, matches.**

### 13.
Adds \(c3\log(\,c4*(c5|A|+1)^{c6}e^{c7 t}+1)\). Nonlinear in \(A\) and extra term. Only removable by \(c3=0\), then #6. **Yes, matches (set \(c3=0\)).**

### 14.
\(A c0 + A c1 e^{c2 t} + c3\log(c4 t+1)|A|^{c5}\). Exponential/log-|A| mix; cannot yield \(A\log(\beta t+1)\) for all \(A\). Even if \(c3=0\), still exponential not log. **No**.

### 15.
